A typical pay table starts with a minimum hand of a pair of jacks, which pays even money. (Multi-play games are offered in \"Triple Play\", \"Five Play\", \"Ten Play\", \"Fifty Play\" and \"One Hundred Play\" versions.) \r\n\r\nIn games which do not have a wild card a player on average will receive the rare four-of-a-kind hand approximately once every 500 hands, while a player may play tens of thousands of hands before an extremely rare royal flush, which usually has the highest payout. \r\n\r\n\"Jacks or Better,\" sometimes simply called \"Draw Poker,\" is the most common variation of video poker.
